[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Stress at work with 7 questions:

**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding how stress affects your work experience. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more supportive work environment.

**1. How often do you feel stressed at work?**

a) Almost never
b) Occasionally (1-2 times a week)
c) Frequently (3-4 times a week)
d) Almost always

**2. What are the most common causes of stress at work for you? (Check all that apply)**

* Tight deadlines
* High workload
* Lack of control over tasks
* Conflicting priorities
* Poor communication with colleagues or management
* Other (please specify)

**3. How do you typically handle stress at work?**

a) Take a break to relax and recharge
b) Try to push through and focus on the task at hand
c) Seek support from colleagues or a supervisor
d) Take a few deep breaths and try to manage my emotions
e) Other (please specify)

**4. Do you feel like your workload is manageable, or do you often feel overwhelmed?**

a) Manageable
b) Sometimes manageable, sometimes overwhelming
c) Often overwhelming
d) Always overwhelming

**5. Have you experienced any physical symptoms of stress at work (e.g. headaches, fatigue, muscle tension)?**

a) Yes, frequently
b) Yes, occasionally
c) No, never

**6. How do you think your workplace could better support your well-being and reduce stress?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide suggestions)

**7. Would you like to receive stress-reduction training or resources at work?**

a) Yes, that would be very helpful
b) Maybe, it depends on the content and format
c) No, I don't think it would be helpful

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and stress-reduced work environment.

Here is a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions:

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your opinion and want to understand your perceptions of our workplace environment. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more comfortable and productive work environment. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**1. How would you rate the overall comfort and cleanliness of our workspace?**

a) Very comfortable and clean
b) Somewhat comfortable and clean
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat uncomfortable and dirty
e) Very uncomfortable and dirty

**2. Do you feel that our workspace is well-organized and easy to navigate?**

a) Yes, it's very easy to find what I need
b) Somewhat easy to find what I need
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat difficult to find what I need
e) Very difficult to find what I need

**3. How would you rate the level of noise and distractions in our workspace?**

a) Very quiet and minimal distractions
b) Somewhat quiet and minimal distractions
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat noisy and distracting
e) Very noisy and distracting

**4. Do you feel that our workspace provides adequate natural light and ventilation?**

a) Yes, it's very bright and well-ventilated
b) Somewhat bright and well-ventilated
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dark and poorly ventilated
e) Very dark and poorly ventilated

**5. How would you rate the quality of our workspace amenities (e.g., break room, kitchen, restrooms)?**

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor
e) Very poor

**6. Do you feel that our workspace is well-suited for collaboration and teamwork?**

a) Yes, it's very conducive to collaboration
b) Somewhat conducive to collaboration
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat challenging to collaborate
e) Very challenging to collaborate

**7. Are there any specific changes or improvements you would like to see in our workspace to make it more comfortable and productive?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide their suggestions)

I hope this helps! Let me know if you need any further assistance.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on End of working relationship with 10 questions:

**End of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** This questionnaire aims to gather your thoughts and experiences regarding the end of a working relationship with a colleague or team member. Your responses will help us understand the reasons, challenges, and outcomes of such situations.

**1. Can you describe the most recent instance where a working relationship with a colleague or team member came to an end? (Open-ended question)**

**2. What was the primary reason for the end of the working relationship? (Select one)**

a) Poor communication
b) Lack of trust
c) Conflicting work styles
d) Performance issues
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How did you feel about the end of the working relationship? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 = Very negative, 5 = Neutral)**

**4. Were there any specific incidents or behaviors that contributed to the end of the working relationship? If so, please describe. (Open-ended question)**

**5. Do you think the organization could have done something to prevent the end of the working relationship? (Select one)**

a) Yes, definitely
b) Maybe
c) No, it was unavoidable
d) I'm not sure

**6. How did the organization handle the end of the working relationship? (Select one)**

a) Professional and respectful
b) Unprofessional and unrespectful
c) Unclear or unclear communication
d) Other (please specify)

**7. Have you experienced any negative consequences or impacts as a result of the end of the working relationship? (Select one)**

a) Yes, significant
b) Yes, minor
c) No, none
d) I'm not sure

**8. How has the end of the working relationship affected your job satisfaction and overall well-being? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 = Very negative, 5 = Neutral)**

**9. Are there any changes or improvements you would suggest the organization make to prevent or manage the end of working relationships in the future? (Open-ended question)**

**10. Is there anything else you would like to share about your experience with the end of a working relationship? (Open-ended question)**

Please note that all responses will be kept confidential and anonymous. Thank you for taking the time to participate in this questionnaire!

* Somewhat satisfied
* Neutral
* Somewhat dissatisfied

* Somewhat important

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We're interested in understanding your perceptions of your career path and how clear you are about your future career goals. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and provide a more tailored support system for your career development.

**1. How would you rate the clarity of your current career goals?**

a) Very clear: I have a specific career path in mind and know what steps I need to take to achieve it.
b) Somewhat clear: I have a general idea of what I want to achieve, but I'm not entirely sure about the specifics.
c) Not very clear: I'm not sure what I want to achieve or where I want to go in my career.
d) Not at all clear: I'm still exploring my options and don't have a clear direction.

**2. What motivates you to pursue your current career goals? (Select all that apply)**

a) Financial stability
b) Job satisfaction
c) Opportunities for growth and development
d) Sense of fulfillment and purpose
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How often do you reflect on your career goals and make adjustments as needed?**

a) Daily/weekly: I regularly take time to reflect on my goals and make adjustments.
b) Monthly: I occasionally take time to reflect on my goals and make adjustments.
c) Quarterly: I take time to reflect on my goals and make adjustments a few times a year.
d) Rarely: I rarely take time to reflect on my goals and make adjustments.

**4. What barriers, if any, do you face in achieving your career goals? (Select all that apply)**

a) Lack of resources (time, money, etc.)
b) Limited networking opportunities
c) Limited access to training or development opportunities
d) Fear of failure or taking risks
e) Other (please specify)

**5. How important is it for you to have a clear career path in the next 2-3 years?**

a) Very important: I need a clear direction to feel motivated and focused.
b) Somewhat important: A clear direction would be helpful, but I can still achieve my goals without one.
c) Not very important: I'm more focused on day-to-day tasks than long-term goals.
d) Not at all important: I'm not concerned with having a clear career path.

**6. Have you received feedback from others that has helped you clarify your career goals? If so, what was the feedback?**

(Open-ended text field for respondents to share their experiences)

**7. How confident are you in your ability to achieve your career goals?**

a) Very confident: I'm certain I can achieve my goals.
b) Somewhat confident: I'm fairly confident, but there are some uncertainties.
c) Not very confident: I'm not sure if I can achieve my goals.
d) Not at all confident: I don't think I can achieve my goals.

**8. What steps do you think would help you achieve your career goals? (Select all that apply)**

a) Mentorship or coaching
b) Training or development opportunities
c) Networking or building relationships
d) Setting specific, measurable goals
e) Other (please specify)

**9. Are there any additional comments or suggestions you'd like to share about your career path clarity?**

(Open-ended text field for respondents to share their thoughts)

**1. How often do you provide feedback to your supervisor or HR department?**

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Quarterly
e) Rarely
f) Never

a) To improve a process or procedure
b) To recognize and reward good work
c) To address a concern or issue
d) To provide suggestions for growth and development
e) Other (please specify)

(Please rank the following options in order of importance to you)

1. Regular one-on-one meetings with supervisor
2. Anonymous feedback forms
3. Online survey tools
4. Performance reviews
5. Other (please specify)

**4. Have you ever received feedback from your supervisor or HR department? If so, how did you feel about it?**

a) Very positive - it helped me grow and improve
b) Somewhat positive - it was useful, but could be improved
c) Neutral - it was just okay
d) Somewhat negative - it was not helpful or constructive
e) Very negative - it was unhelpful or hurtful

**5. What do you think is the most important aspect of a feedback mechanism?**

(Please select one of the following options)

a) Timeliness - receiving feedback in a timely manner
b) Transparency - knowing who is providing the feedback and why
c) Constructiveness - receiving feedback that is helpful and actionable
d) Anonymity - having the option to provide feedback anonymously
e) Other (please specify)

**6. Have you ever had a suggestion or idea implemented as a result of providing feedback? If so, what was the outcome?**

**7. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about our feedback mechanisms?**

(Please use the space provided to provide any additional thoughts or ideas you may have)

* Never

* Clear and concise
* Open and transparent
* Inconsistent or unclear
* Non-existent or unresponsive

* Yes, but it was not specific or actionable

* Medium - I trust them, but have some reservations
* Low - I do not trust or respect them

* Yes, occasionally
* No, rarely or never

* Very satisfied
* Somewhat satisfied
* Neutral
* Somewhat dissatisfied
* Very dissatisfied

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** As part of our ongoing efforts to improve leadership development, we would like to gather your feedback on the effectiveness of our leaders. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and opportunities for growth. Please answer the following questions honestly and to the best of your ability.

**1. How would you rate the overall leadership style of your supervisor/manager?**

a) Excellent - always sets clear goals and expectations
b) Good - generally effective, but could improve in certain areas
c) Fair - sometimes effective, but inconsistent
d) Poor - often unclear or unresponsive

**2. How often do you feel motivated and inspired by your leader's vision and direction?**

a) Almost always - my leader's vision is clear and compelling
b) Most of the time - my leader's vision is generally clear, but not always inspiring
c) Sometimes - my leader's vision is unclear or uninspiring
d) Rarely - my leader's vision is not motivating or inspiring

**3. How would you rate the level of trust and confidence you have in your leader's decision-making?**

a) High - I fully trust my leader's judgment
b) Medium - I generally trust my leader's judgment, but have some reservations
c) Low - I have significant doubts about my leader's judgment

**4. How would you rate the level of communication and feedback from your leader?**

a) Excellent - regular, clear, and constructive feedback
b) Good - generally good communication, but could be more regular
c) Fair - occasional, but not always clear or constructive feedback
d) Poor - infrequent, unclear, or unconstructive feedback

**5. How would you rate the level of support and resources provided by your leader to help you achieve your goals?**

a) Excellent - always available and willing to help
b) Good - generally supportive, but sometimes unavailable
c) Fair - sometimes supportive, but not always available
d) Poor - rarely supportive or unavailable

**6. How would you rate the level of accountability and consequences for underperformance or mistakes?**

a) High - clear consequences and accountability for underperformance
b) Medium - generally clear consequences, but some ambiguity
c) Low - unclear consequences or lack of accountability

**7. How likely are you to recommend your leader to others, or to seek out their leadership in the future?**

a) Very likely - I highly recommend my leader
b) Likely - I would recommend my leader, but with some reservations
c) Not very likely - I would not recommend my leader, but might consider in the future
d) Not at all likely - I would not recommend my leader

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Onboarding Experience with 6 questions:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

We want to hear about your experience during the onboarding process at our company. Your feedback will help us improve and refine our onboarding process to better support new hires. Please answer the following questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions at the end.

1. **How would you rate your overall onboarding experience?**

a) Excellent - I felt well-prepared and supported throughout the process.
b) Good - I had some minor issues, but overall it was a positive experience.
c) Fair - I had some challenges, but I was able to adjust and adapt.
d) Poor - I struggled to find my footing, and it took me a while to get up to speed.

2. **What was the most helpful aspect of the onboarding process for you?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide specific feedback)

3. **Were you introduced to the right people and resources during onboarding?**

a) Yes, I felt like I had a good understanding of who to reach out to and what resources were available.
b) Mostly, but I had to seek out additional information or clarification.
c) Not really - I had to figure things out on my own or rely on colleagues for help.
d) No, I didn't have a clear understanding of who to turn to or what resources were available.

4. **How would you rate the quality of the training and orientation provided during onboarding?**

a) Excellent - I felt thoroughly prepared for my role and responsibilities.
b) Good - The training was informative, but I had to supplement with additional learning.
c) Fair - The training was adequate, but I had to rely on colleagues for guidance.
d) Poor - The training was inadequate, and I struggled to understand my role and responsibilities.

5. **Did you feel like your manager and team were supportive during the onboarding process?**

a) Yes, I felt like I had a strong support system.
b) Mostly - my manager and team were helpful, but I had to seek out additional support.
c) Not really - I had to rely on colleagues or other resources for support.
d) No, I didn't feel like I had a supportive manager or team.

6. **What changes would you suggest to improve the onboarding experience for future new hires?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide specific feedback and suggestions)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our onboarding process.

**Pressure at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding your experiences and perceptions of pressure at work. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve our work environment and support your well-being.

**Section 1: General Perceptions**

1. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

	* Strongly agree, somewhat agree, neither agree nor disagree, somewhat disagree, strongly disagree

	* Very high, high, moderate, low, very low

**Section 2: Causes of Pressure**

	* Unrealistic expectations from management or colleagues
	* Lack of resources or support
	* High stakes or consequences for mistakes
	* Constant change or uncertainty
	* Other (please specify)

	* Always, most of the time, sometimes, rarely, never

	* Yes, often; yes, sometimes; no

	* Always, most of the time, sometimes, rarely, never

**Section 4: Coping Mechanisms**

	* Prioritize tasks and focus on one thing at a time

	* Other (please specify)

	* Strongly agree, somewhat agree, neither agree nor disagree, somewhat disagree, strongly disagree

	* (Open-ended text field)

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

* Read industry publications and articles

* Improved job performance and skills
* Increased earning potential

**Introduction:** We value your well-being and want to understand how you manage your work and personal life. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more balanced work environment.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Workplace Culture with 6 questions:

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value the unique culture that exists within our organization and want to hear from you about your experiences and perceptions. Your input will help us understand what we're doing well and where we can improve. Please answer the following questions honestly and to the best of your ability.

**1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at our workplace?**

* Is it collaborative and supportive, or more competitive and individualistic?
* Are there opportunities for socialization and building relationships with colleagues?
* Are there any specific events, traditions, or rituals that contribute to this atmosphere?

**2. How do you think our organization's values and mission are reflected in daily work?**

* Do you feel like your work aligns with the organization's values and mission?
* Are there any specific practices or behaviors that demonstrate these values?
* Are there any areas where you feel like the organization's values and mission are not being upheld?

**3. How do you typically handle conflicts or disagreements with colleagues?**

* Do you tend to address them directly and openly, or do you try to avoid them?
* Are there any specific processes or procedures that help resolve conflicts?
* Are there any instances where you felt like a conflict was not addressed effectively?

**4. What do you think are the most important factors that contribute to a positive and productive work environment?**

* Is it the physical workspace, the people you work with, or something else?
* Are there any specific perks, benefits, or amenities that make your workday more enjoyable?
* Are there any areas where you feel like the organization could improve to enhance your work experience?

**5. How do you feel about the level of transparency and communication within our organization?**

* Do you feel like you receive timely and accurate information about changes or updates?
* Are there any specific channels or methods that you prefer for communication?
* Are there any instances where you felt like information was not shared effectively or in a timely manner?

**6. What suggestions do you have for improving our workplace culture?**

* Is there a specific policy, practice, or program that you think would make a positive impact?
* Are there any changes you would like to see in terms of leadership, management, or employee engagement?
* Are there any areas where you feel like the organization is already excelling, and what can be done to build on that success?

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and opinions! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand and improve our workplace culture.

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value the unique culture that makes our workplace special. Your feedback will help us understand what we're doing well and where we can improve. Your responses will be kept confidential.

**1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere in our workplace?**

a) Friendly and collaborative
b) Professional and formal
c) Casual and relaxed
d) Other (please specify)

**2. To what extent do you feel like you belong and are valued in our workplace?**

a) Strongly agree - I feel like I'm part of the team
b) Somewhat agree - I feel like I'm a valued contributor
c) Neither agree nor disagree - I'm neutral
d) Somewhat disagree - I feel like I'm not fully included
e) Strongly disagree - I feel like I don't belong

**3. How often do you experience a sense of camaraderie with your colleagues?**

a) Almost always
b) Often
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely
e) Never

**4. What do you think is the most important aspect of our workplace culture? (Check all that apply)**

a) Sense of community
b) Flexibility and work-life balance
c) Recognition and rewards
d) Open communication and feedback
e) Other (please specify)

**5. Have you ever felt uncomfortable or hesitant to speak up or share your ideas in our workplace?**

a) Yes, often
b) Yes, sometimes
c) Rarely
d) Never

**6. How would you rate the level of trust and respect among team members?**

a) Very high - we trust and respect each other
b) Somewhat high - we generally trust and respect each other
c) Neutral - it's a mixed bag
d) Somewhat low - we sometimes struggle with trust and respect
e) Very low - we often struggle with trust and respect

**7. What changes would you like to see in our workplace culture to make it more enjoyable and fulfilling? (Open-ended question)**

**8. Any additional comments or suggestions about our workplace culture? (Open-ended question)**

**2. How often do you feel comfortable taking breaks or stepping away from your desk to recharge?**

a) Almost always - I feel comfortable taking breaks whenever I need to
b) Most of the time - I feel comfortable taking breaks, but sometimes feel guilty or worried about falling behind
c) Some of the time - I feel uncomfortable taking breaks, but try to do so occasionally
d) Rarely - I rarely take breaks and feel like I'm always "on the clock"

**5. How would you rate the overall sense of community and camaraderie among colleagues in your department?**

b) Good - we have a decent sense of community and camaraderie, but room for improvement
c) Fair - we have some sense of community and camaraderie, but it's not always strong
d) Poor - we don't have a strong sense of community and camaraderie

**6. Are there any specific changes or improvements you would like to see in our workplace environment?**

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your opinion and want to understand how you perceive our workplace environment. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a better work environment for everyone. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**1. How would you rate the overall comfort and cleanliness of your workspace?**

a) Very comfortable and clean
b) Somewhat comfortable and clean
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat uncomfortable and dirty
e) Very uncomfortable and dirty

**2. Do you feel that your workspace is well-lit and has adequate ventilation?**

a) Yes, it is well-lit and has good ventilation
b) Mostly, but there's room for improvement
c) Neutral
d) No, it's not well-lit or ventilated well
e) Not applicable (I don't spend much time in my workspace)

**3. How often do you feel stressed or overwhelmed at work?**

a) Rarely
b) Occasionally
c) Frequently
d) Almost always
e) Always

**4. Are there sufficient resources and equipment available to you to perform your job effectively?**

a) Yes, I have all the resources I need
b) Mostly, but I sometimes have to wait for equipment or supplies
c) Neutral
d) No, I often have to go without or find alternative solutions
e) Not applicable (my job doesn't require specific resources)

**5. Do you feel that your workplace is inclusive and welcoming to all employees, regardless of their background or identity?**

a) Yes, I feel included and welcome
b) Mostly, but there are some areas for improvement
c) Neutral
d) No, I don't feel included or welcome
e) Not applicable (I'm not sure or don't have personal experience)

**6. How would you rate the level of noise and distractions in your workspace?**

a) Very quiet and minimal distractions
b) Somewhat quiet, but with occasional distractions
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat noisy and distracting
e) Very noisy and distracting

**7. Are there opportunities for socialization and team-building within the workplace?**

a) Yes, there are regular team-building activities and social events
b) Mostly, but I don't always participate
c) Neutral
d) No, there aren't many opportunities for socialization
e) Not applicable (I don't participate in team-building activities)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions:

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your opinion and would like to understand your perception of our workplace environment. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a better work environment for everyone.

**Please answer the following questions:**

1. **Overall Satisfaction:** How satisfied are you with the physical workspace (e.g., lighting, temperature, noise level, cleanliness)?

a) Very Satisfied
b) Somewhat Satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat Dissatisfied
e) Very Dissatisfied

2. **Collaboration Spaces:** How often do you use shared spaces (e.g., meeting rooms, break rooms, collaboration areas) for work or socializing?

a) Daily
b) Several times a week
c) Occasionally
d) Rarely
e) Never

3. **Noise Levels:** How would you rate the noise levels in your workspace?

a) Quiet and comfortable
b) Moderate - some background noise
c) Loud and distracting
d) Unpredictable - varies throughout the day

4. **Lighting:** How would you rate the lighting in your workspace?

a) Bright and comfortable
b) Adequate - some areas could be brighter
c) Dim - could use more light
d) Unpredictable - varies throughout the day

5. **Work-Life Balance:** Do you feel that your work schedule and expectations allow for a healthy work-life balance?

a) Yes, definitely
b) Mostly, but sometimes it's challenging
c) Somewhat, but could be better
d) No, it's difficult to maintain a balance

6. **Wellness Initiatives:** Are you aware of and take advantage of wellness initiatives (e.g., exercise classes, mental health resources, healthy snack options)?

a) Yes, I'm very aware and take advantage
b) Somewhat aware, but don't use the resources
c) Not very aware, but might use them
d) Not at all aware

7. **Suggestions for Improvement:** What changes would you like to see in our workplace environment to improve your overall experience?

(Open-ended text box for respondents to provide their suggestions)

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts on our workplace environment! Your input is invaluable to us.
